\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SizeConstraintRect}{SizeConstraintRect}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a} 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Defines to which rect of a layout element the size constraints that can be set via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{set\+Minimum\+Size} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{set\+Maximum\+Size} apply. The outer rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}) includes the margins (e.\+g. in the case of a \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect}{QCPAxis\+Rect} the axis labels), whereas the inner rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect}) does not.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a792e1f3d9cb1591fca135bb0de9b81fc_a792e1f3d9cb1591fca135bb0de9b81fc}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!addAxes@{addAxes}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addAxes()}{addAxes()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a792e1f3d9cb1591fca135bb0de9b81fc_a792e1f3d9cb1591fca135bb0de9b81fc} 
QList$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_axis}{QCPAxis}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} $>$ QCPAxis\+Rect\+::add\+Axes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QCPAxis\+::\+Axis\+Types}]{types}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Adds a new axis with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a2a845ee60eac7a8d5e71718c5e77c274_a2a845ee60eac7a8d5e71718c5e77c274}{add\+Axis} to each axis rect side specified in {\itshape types}. This may be an {\ttfamily or}-\/combination of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_ae2bcc1728b382f10f064612b368bc18a_ae2bcc1728b382f10f064612b368bc18a}{QCPAxis\+::\+Axis\+Type}, so axes can be added to multiple sides at once.

Returns a list of the added axes.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a2a845ee60eac7a8d5e71718c5e77c274_a2a845ee60eac7a8d5e71718c5e77c274}{add\+Axis}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a5fa906175447b14206954f77fc7f1ef4_a5fa906175447b14206954f77fc7f1ef4}{setup\+Full\+Axes\+Box}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a2a845ee60eac7a8d5e71718c5e77c274_a2a845ee60eac7a8d5e71718c5e77c274}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!addAxis@{addAxis}}
\index{addAxis@{addAxis}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addAxis()}{addAxis()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a2a845ee60eac7a8d5e71718c5e77c274_a2a845ee60eac7a8d5e71718c5e77c274} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_axis}{QCPAxis}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} QCPAxis\+Rect\+::add\+Axis (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_axis_ae2bcc1728b382f10f064612b368bc18a_ae2bcc1728b382f10f064612b368bc18a}{QCPAxis\+::\+Axis\+Type}}}]{type}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_axis}{QCPAxis}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{axis}{ = {\ttfamily nullptr}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Adds a new axis to the axis rect side specified with {\itshape type}, and returns it. If {\itshape axis} is 0, a new \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis}{QCPAxis} instance is created internally. \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} owns the returned axis, so if you want to remove an axis, use \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a03c39cd9704f0d36fb6cf980cdddcbaa_a03c39cd9704f0d36fb6cf980cdddcbaa}{remove\+Axis} instead of deleting it manually.

You may inject \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis}{QCPAxis} instances (or subclasses of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis}{QCPAxis}) by setting {\itshape axis} to an axis that was previously created outside \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot}. It is important to note that \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} takes ownership of the axis, so you may not delete it afterwards. Further, the {\itshape axis} must have been created with this axis rect as parent and with the same axis type as specified in {\itshape type}. If this is not the case, a debug output is generated, the axis is not added, and the method returns {\ttfamily nullptr}.

This method can not be used to move {\itshape axis} between axis rects. The same {\itshape axis} instance must not be added multiple times to the same or different axis rects.

If an axis rect side already contains one or more axes, the lower and upper endings of the new axis (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_a08af1c72db9ae4dc8cb8a973d44405ab_a08af1c72db9ae4dc8cb8a973d44405ab}{QCPAxis\+::set\+Lower\+Ending}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_a69119b892fc306f651763596685aa377_a69119b892fc306f651763596685aa377}{QCPAxis\+::set\+Upper\+Ending}) are set to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_line_ending_a5ef16e6876b4b74959c7261d8d4c2cd5_a5ef16e6876b4b74959c7261d8d4c2cd5a126c390f0c359fcd8df1fc5e38d26d5b}{QCPLine\+Ending\+::es\+Half\+Bar}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a792e1f3d9cb1591fca135bb0de9b81fc_a792e1f3d9cb1591fca135bb0de9b81fc}{add\+Axes}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a5fa906175447b14206954f77fc7f1ef4_a5fa906175447b14206954f77fc7f1ef4}{setup\+Full\+Axes\+Box} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a3aee067fd105f2fa8de9eb8024435ac5_a3aee067fd105f2fa8de9eb8024435ac5} 
QList$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} $>$ QCPAxis\+Rect\+::elements (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{recursive}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns a list of all child elements in this layout element. If {\itshape recursive} is true, all sub-\/child elements are included in the list, too.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
There may be {\ttfamily nullptr} entries in the returned list. For example, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid}{QCPLayout\+Grid} may have empty cells which yield {\ttfamily nullptr} at the respective index. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{maximumOuterSizeHint()}{maximumOuterSizeHint()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_ad96efb977a26e360e8a64a4c1e56456d_ad96efb977a26e360e8a64a4c1e56456d} 
QSize QCPLayout\+Element\+::maximum\+Outer\+Size\+Hint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the suggested maximum size this layout element (the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}) may be expanded to, if no manual maximum size is set.

if a maximum size (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{set\+Maximum\+Size}) was not set manually, parent layouts use the returned size (usually indirectly through \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_add49fd6843821a6126914b837ed52e22_add49fd6843821a6126914b837ed52e22}{QCPLayout\+::get\+Final\+Maximum\+Outer\+Size}) to determine the maximum allowed size of this layout element.

A manual maximum size is considered set if it is smaller than Qt\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily QWIDGETSIZE\+\_\+\+MAX}.

The default implementation simply returns {\ttfamily QWIDGETSIZE\+\_\+\+MAX} for both width and height, implying no suggested maximum size. Reimplementations may use their detailed knowledge about the layout element\textquotesingle{}s content to provide size hints. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a41ce0014c220d77b909e2ca937f0e599_a41ce0014c220d77b909e2ca937f0e599}{QCPLayout\+Grid}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_text_element_ae82475b50c10a5b3314d996d50ae536b_ae82475b50c10a5b3314d996d50ae536b}{QCPText\+Element}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a46789036c4fcb190fa374f91321d7c09_a46789036c4fcb190fa374f91321d7c09} 
QSize QCPLayout\+Element\+::minimum\+Outer\+Size\+Hint (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the suggested minimum size this layout element (the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}) may be compressed to, if no manual minimum size is set.

if a minimum size (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{set\+Minimum\+Size}) was not set manually, parent layouts use the returned size (usually indirectly through \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_a864fddc84721f186663faf3683f1fa70_a864fddc84721f186663faf3683f1fa70}{QCPLayout\+::get\+Final\+Minimum\+Outer\+Size}) to determine the minimum allowed size of this layout element.

A manual minimum size is considered set if it is non-\/zero.

The default implementation simply returns the sum of the horizontal margins for the width and the sum of the vertical margins for the height. Reimplementations may use their detailed knowledge about the layout element\textquotesingle{}s content to provide size hints. 

Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_grid_a0438bc58b4d3894d01db95b08d4268df_a0438bc58b4d3894d01db95b08d4268df}{QCPLayout\+Grid}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_plottable_legend_item_a8b543f3ac32b2fe59326e01c1101b3b8_a8b543f3ac32b2fe59326e01c1101b3b8}{QCPPlottable\+Legend\+Item}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_polar_legend_item_a17e2c0da8308a014b1d4339131215217_a17e2c0da8308a014b1d4339131215217}{QCPPolar\+Legend\+Item}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_text_element_a47b8541f55ff520c557e0f27461f109e_a47b8541f55ff520c557e0f27461f109e}{QCPText\+Element}}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!mouseDoubleClickEvent@{mouseDoubleClickEvent}}
\index{mouseDoubleClickEvent@{mouseDoubleClickEvent}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseDoubleClickEvent()}{mouseDoubleClickEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81} 
void QCPLayerable\+::mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QMouse\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{, }\item[{const QVariant \&}]{details}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

This event gets called when the user presses the mouse button a second time in a double-\/click, while the cursor is over the layerable. Whether a cursor is over the layerable is decided by a preceding call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c}{select\+Test}.

The \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event} is called instead of the second \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{mouse\+Press\+Event}. So in the case of a double-\/click, the event succession is {\itshape press\+Event -- release\+Event -- double\+Click\+Event -- release\+Event}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}. The parameter {\itshape details} contains layerable-\/specific details about the hit, which were generated in the previous call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c}{select\+Test}. For example, One-\/dimensional plottables like \doxylink{class_q_c_p_graph}{QCPGraph} or \doxylink{class_q_c_p_bars}{QCPBars} convey the clicked data point in the {\itshape details} parameter, as \doxylink{class_q_c_p_data_selection}{QCPData\+Selection} packed as QVariant. Multi-\/part objects convey the specific {\ttfamily Selectable\+Part} that was hit (e.\+g. \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_abee4c7a54c468b1385dfce2c898b115f_abee4c7a54c468b1385dfce2c898b115f}{QCPAxis\+::\+Selectable\+Part} in the case of axes).

Similarly to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, once a layerable has accepted the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event}, it is considered the mouse grabber and will receive all following calls to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb}{mouse\+Move\+Event} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4}{mouse\+Release\+Event} for this mouse interaction (a "{}mouse interaction"{} in this context ends with the release).

The default implementation does nothing except explicitly ignoring the event with {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}ignore()}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb}{mouse\+Move\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4}{mouse\+Release\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a93eeaa0c127d6d6fe8171b2455080262_a93eeaa0c127d6d6fe8171b2455080262}{wheel\+Event} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Reimplemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_text_element_a2272ff775ab385f612e9fd39773de7c0_a2272ff775ab385f612e9fd39773de7c0}{QCPText\+Element}}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!mouseMoveEvent@{mouseMoveEvent}}
\index{mouseMoveEvent@{mouseMoveEvent}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseMoveEvent()}{mouseMoveEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::mouse\+Move\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QMouse\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{, }\item[{const QPointF \&}]{start\+Pos}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

This event gets called when the user moves the mouse while holding a mouse button, after this layerable has become the mouse grabber by accepting the preceding \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{mouse\+Press\+Event}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}. The parameter {\itshape start\+Pos} indicates the position where the initial \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{mouse\+Press\+Event} occurred, that started the mouse interaction.

The default implementation does nothing.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4}{mouse\+Release\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a93eeaa0c127d6d6fe8171b2455080262_a93eeaa0c127d6d6fe8171b2455080262}{wheel\+Event} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


Reimplemented from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb}{QCPAxis\+Rect}}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!mousePressEvent@{mousePressEvent}}
\index{mousePressEvent@{mousePressEvent}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mousePressEvent()}{mousePressEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::mouse\+Press\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QMouse\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{, }\item[{const QVariant \&}]{details}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

This event gets called when the user presses a mouse button while the cursor is over the layerable. Whether a cursor is over the layerable is decided by a preceding call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c}{select\+Test}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}. The parameter {\itshape details} contains layerable-\/specific details about the hit, which were generated in the previous call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c}{select\+Test}. For example, One-\/dimensional plottables like \doxylink{class_q_c_p_graph}{QCPGraph} or \doxylink{class_q_c_p_bars}{QCPBars} convey the clicked data point in the {\itshape details} parameter, as \doxylink{class_q_c_p_data_selection}{QCPData\+Selection} packed as QVariant. Multi-\/part objects convey the specific {\ttfamily Selectable\+Part} that was hit (e.\+g. \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_abee4c7a54c468b1385dfce2c898b115f_abee4c7a54c468b1385dfce2c898b115f}{QCPAxis\+::\+Selectable\+Part} in the case of axes).

\doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} uses an event propagation system that works the same as Qt\textquotesingle{}s system. If your layerable doesn\textquotesingle{}t reimplement the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{mouse\+Press\+Event} or explicitly calls {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}ignore()} in its reimplementation, the event will be propagated to the next layerable in the stacking order.

Once a layerable has accepted the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, it is considered the mouse grabber and will receive all following calls to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb}{mouse\+Move\+Event} or \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4}{mouse\+Release\+Event} for this mouse interaction (a "{}mouse interaction"{} in this context ends with the release).

The default implementation does nothing except explicitly ignoring the event with {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}ignore()}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb}{mouse\+Move\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4}{mouse\+Release\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a93eeaa0c127d6d6fe8171b2455080262_a93eeaa0c127d6d6fe8171b2455080262}{wheel\+Event} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{mouseReleaseEvent@{mouseReleaseEvent}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mouseReleaseEvent()}{mouseReleaseEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::mouse\+Release\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QMouse\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{, }\item[{const QPointF \&}]{start\+Pos}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

This event gets called when the user releases the mouse button, after this layerable has become the mouse grabber by accepting the preceding \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{mouse\+Press\+Event}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}. The parameter {\itshape start\+Pos} indicates the position where the initial \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{mouse\+Press\+Event} occurred, that started the mouse interaction.

The default implementation does nothing.

\doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb}{mouse\+Move\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a93eeaa0c127d6d6fe8171b2455080262_a93eeaa0c127d6d6fe8171b2455080262}{wheel\+Event} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!outerRect@{outerRect}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{outerRect()}{outerRect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c} 
QRect QCPLayout\+Element\+::outer\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the outer rect of this layout element. The outer rect is the inner rect expanded by the margins (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf}{set\+Margins}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins}). The outer rect is used (and set via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f}{set\+Outer\+Rect}) by the parent \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout}{QCPLayout} to control the size of this layout element.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layerable_aa78b7e644d2c519e1a9a6f2ac5fcd858_aa78b7e644d2c519e1a9a6f2ac5fcd858}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!parentLayerable@{parentLayerable}}
\index{parentLayerable@{parentLayerable}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{parentLayerable()}{parentLayerable()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layerable_aa78b7e644d2c519e1a9a6f2ac5fcd858_aa78b7e644d2c519e1a9a6f2ac5fcd858} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layerable}{QCPLayerable}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} QCPLayerable\+::parent\+Layerable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the parent layerable of this layerable. The parent layerable is used to provide visibility hierarchies in conjunction with the method \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7}{real\+Visibility}. This way, layerables only get drawn if their parent layerables are visible, too.

Note that a parent layerable is not necessarily also the QObject parent for memory management. Further, a layerable doesn\textquotesingle{}t always have a parent layerable, so this function may return {\ttfamily nullptr}.

A parent layerable is set implicitly when placed inside layout elements and doesn\textquotesingle{}t need to be set manually by the user. Here is the caller graph for this function\+:\nopagebreak
\begin{figure}[H]
\begin{center}
\leavevmode

\end{center}
\end{figure}

Returns a list of all the plottables that are associated with this axis rect.

A plottable is considered associated with an axis rect if its key or value axis (or both) is in this axis rect.

bool QCPLayerable\+::real\+Visibility (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns whether this layerable is visible, taking the visibility of the layerable parent and the visibility of this layerable\textquotesingle{}s layer into account. This is the method that is consulted to decide whether a layerable shall be drawn or not.

If this layerable has a direct layerable parent (usually set via hierarchies implemented in subclasses, like in the case of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element}), this function returns true only if this layerable has its visibility set to true and the parent layerable\textquotesingle{}s \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7_ab054e88f15d485defcb95e7376f119e7}{real\+Visibility} returns true. \index{rect@{rect}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rect()}{rect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4} 
QRect QCPLayout\+Element\+::rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Returns the inner rect of this layout element. The inner rect is the outer rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f}{set\+Outer\+Rect}) shrinked by the margins (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf}{set\+Margins}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins}).

In some cases, the area between outer and inner rect is left blank. In other cases the margin area is used to display peripheral graphics while the main content is in the inner rect. This is where automatic margin calculation becomes interesting because it allows the layout element to adapt the margins to the peripheral graphics it wants to draw. For example, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect}{QCPAxis\+Rect} draws the axis labels and tick labels in the margin area, thus needs to adjust the margins (if \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins} is enabled) according to the space required by the labels of the axes.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\end{center}
\end{figure}

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!selectTest@{selectTest}}
\index{selectTest@{selectTest}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{selectTest()}{selectTest()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c} 
double QCPLayout\+Element\+::select\+Test (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QPointF \&}]{pos}{, }\item[{bool}]{only\+Selectable}{, }\item[{QVariant \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{details}{ = {\ttfamily nullptr}}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}, {\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Layout elements are sensitive to events inside their outer rect. If {\itshape pos} is within the outer rect, this method returns a value corresponding to 0.\+99 times the parent plot\textquotesingle{}s selection tolerance. However, layout elements are not selectable by default. So if {\itshape only\+Selectable} is true, -\/1.\+0 is returned.

See \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a272989087fc8c4357b4ba614f9922336_a272989087fc8c4357b4ba614f9922336}{QCPLayerable\+::select\+Test} for a general explanation of this virtual method.

\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element}{QCPLayout\+Element} subclasses may reimplement this method to provide more specific selection test behaviour. 

Reimplemented from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a272989087fc8c4357b4ba614f9922336_a272989087fc8c4357b4ba614f9922336}{QCPLayerable}}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!setAutoMargins@{setAutoMargins}}
\index{setAutoMargins@{setAutoMargins}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setAutoMargins()}{setAutoMargins()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Auto\+Margins (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QCP\+::\+Margin\+Sides}]{sides}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets on which sides the margin shall be calculated automatically. If a side is calculated automatically, a minimum margin value may be provided with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0a8a17abc16b7923159fcc7608f94673_a0a8a17abc16b7923159fcc7608f94673}{set\+Minimum\+Margins}. If a side is set to be controlled manually, the value may be specified with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf}{set\+Margins}.

Margin sides that are under automatic control may participate in a \doxylink{class_q_c_p_margin_group}{QCPMargin\+Group} (see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a516e56f76b6bc100e8e71d329866847d_a516e56f76b6bc100e8e71d329866847d}{set\+Margin\+Group}), to synchronize (align) it with other layout elements in the plot.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0a8a17abc16b7923159fcc7608f94673_a0a8a17abc16b7923159fcc7608f94673}{set\+Minimum\+Margins}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf}{set\+Margins}, \doxylink{namespace_q_c_p_a7e487e3e2ccb62ab7771065bab7cae54_a7e487e3e2ccb62ab7771065bab7cae54}{QCP\+::\+Margin\+Side} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a22a22b8668735438dc06f9a55fe46b33_a22a22b8668735438dc06f9a55fe46b33}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!setBackground@{setBackground}}
\index{setBackground@{setBackground}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBackground()}{setBackground()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a22a22b8668735438dc06f9a55fe46b33_a22a22b8668735438dc06f9a55fe46b33} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::set\+Background (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QBrush \&}]{brush}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

Sets {\itshape brush} as the background brush. The axis rect background will be filled with this brush. Since axis rects place themselves on the "{}background"{} layer by default, the axis rect backgrounds are usually drawn below everything else.

The brush will be drawn before (under) any background pixmap, which may be specified with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5}{set\+Background(const QPixmap \&pm)}.

To disable drawing of a background brush, set {\itshape brush} to Qt\+::\+No\+Brush.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5}{set\+Background(const QPixmap \&pm)} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!setBackground@{setBackground}}
\index{setBackground@{setBackground}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBackground()}{setBackground()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::set\+Background (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QPixmap \&}]{pm}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets {\itshape pm} as the axis background pixmap. The axis background pixmap will be drawn inside the axis rect. Since axis rects place themselves on the "{}background"{} layer by default, the axis rect backgrounds are usually drawn below everything else.

For cases where the provided pixmap doesn\textquotesingle{}t have the same size as the axis rect, scaling can be enabled with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_ae6d36c3e0e968ffb991170a018e7b503_ae6d36c3e0e968ffb991170a018e7b503}{set\+Background\+Scaled} and the scaling mode (i.\+e. whether and how the aspect ratio is preserved) can be set with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a5ef77ea829c9de7ba248e473f48f7305_a5ef77ea829c9de7ba248e473f48f7305}{set\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode}. To set all these options in one call, consider using the overloaded version of this function.

Below the pixmap, the axis rect may be optionally filled with a brush, if specified with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a22a22b8668735438dc06f9a55fe46b33_a22a22b8668735438dc06f9a55fe46b33}{set\+Background(const QBrush \&brush)}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_ae6d36c3e0e968ffb991170a018e7b503_ae6d36c3e0e968ffb991170a018e7b503}{set\+Background\+Scaled}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a5ef77ea829c9de7ba248e473f48f7305_a5ef77ea829c9de7ba248e473f48f7305}{set\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a22a22b8668735438dc06f9a55fe46b33_a22a22b8668735438dc06f9a55fe46b33}{set\+Background(const QBrush \&brush)} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_ac48a2d5d9b7732e73b86605c69c5e4c1_ac48a2d5d9b7732e73b86605c69c5e4c1}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!setBackground@{setBackground}}
\index{setBackground@{setBackground}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_ac48a2d5d9b7732e73b86605c69c5e4c1_ac48a2d5d9b7732e73b86605c69c5e4c1} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::set\+Background (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QPixmap \&}]{pm}{, }\item[{bool}]{scaled}{, }\item[{Qt\+::\+Aspect\+Ratio\+Mode}]{mode}{ = {\ttfamily Qt\+:\+:KeepAspectRatioByExpanding}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

Allows setting the background pixmap of the axis rect, whether it shall be scaled and how it shall be scaled in one call.

\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_ae6d36c3e0e968ffb991170a018e7b503_ae6d36c3e0e968ffb991170a018e7b503}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!setBackgroundScaled@{setBackgroundScaled}}
\index{setBackgroundScaled@{setBackgroundScaled}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBackgroundScaled()}{setBackgroundScaled()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_ae6d36c3e0e968ffb991170a018e7b503_ae6d36c3e0e968ffb991170a018e7b503} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::set\+Background\+Scaled (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{scaled}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets whether the axis background pixmap shall be scaled to fit the axis rect or not. If {\itshape scaled} is set to true, you may control whether and how the aspect ratio of the original pixmap is preserved with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a5ef77ea829c9de7ba248e473f48f7305_a5ef77ea829c9de7ba248e473f48f7305}{set\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode}.

Note that the scaled version of the original pixmap is buffered, so there is no performance penalty on replots. (Except when the axis rect dimensions are changed continuously.)

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5}{set\+Background}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a5ef77ea829c9de7ba248e473f48f7305_a5ef77ea829c9de7ba248e473f48f7305}{set\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a5ef77ea829c9de7ba248e473f48f7305_a5ef77ea829c9de7ba248e473f48f7305}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!setBackgroundScaledMode@{setBackgroundScaledMode}}
\index{setBackgroundScaledMode@{setBackgroundScaledMode}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setBackgroundScaledMode()}{setBackgroundScaledMode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a5ef77ea829c9de7ba248e473f48f7305_a5ef77ea829c9de7ba248e473f48f7305} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::set\+Background\+Scaled\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Qt\+::\+Aspect\+Ratio\+Mode}]{mode}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

If scaling of the axis background pixmap is enabled (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_ae6d36c3e0e968ffb991170a018e7b503_ae6d36c3e0e968ffb991170a018e7b503}{set\+Background\+Scaled}), use this function to define whether and how the aspect ratio of the original pixmap passed to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5}{set\+Background} is preserved. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5_af615ab5e52b8e0a9a0eff415b6559db5}{set\+Background}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_ae6d36c3e0e968ffb991170a018e7b503_ae6d36c3e0e968ffb991170a018e7b503}{set\+Background\+Scaled} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a516e56f76b6bc100e8e71d329866847d_a516e56f76b6bc100e8e71d329866847d} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Margin\+Group (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QCP\+::\+Margin\+Sides}]{sides}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_margin_group}{QCPMargin\+Group}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{group}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the margin {\itshape group} of the specified margin {\itshape sides}.

Margin groups allow synchronizing specified margins across layout elements, see the documentation of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_margin_group}{QCPMargin\+Group}.

To unset the margin group of {\itshape sides}, set {\itshape group} to {\ttfamily nullptr}.

Note that margin groups only work for margin sides that are set to automatic (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins}).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setMargins()}{setMargins()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf_a8f450b1f3f992ad576fce2c63d8b79cf} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Margins (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QMargins \&}]{margins}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the margins of this layout element. If \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins} is disabled for some or all sides, this function is used to manually set the margin on those sides. Sides that are still set to be handled automatically are ignored and may have any value in {\itshape margins}.

The margin is the distance between the outer rect (controlled by the parent layout via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f}{set\+Outer\+Rect}) and the inner \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} (which usually contains the main content of this layout element).

void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Minimum\+Margins (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QMargins \&}]{margins}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

If \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins} is enabled on some or all margins, this function is used to provide minimum values for those margins.

The minimum values are not enforced on margin sides that were set to be under manual control via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d_accfda49994e3e6d51ed14504abf9d27d}{set\+Auto\+Margins}.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!setMinimumSize@{setMinimumSize}}
\index{setMinimumSize@{setMinimumSize}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setMinimumSize()}{setMinimumSize()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Minimum\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QSize \&}]{size}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the minimum size of this layout element. A parent layout tries to respect the {\itshape size} here by changing row/column sizes in the layout accordingly.

If the parent layout size is not sufficient to satisfy all minimum size constraints of its child layout elements, the layout may set a size that is actually smaller than {\itshape size}. \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} propagates the layout\textquotesingle{}s size constraints to the outside by setting its own minimum QWidget size accordingly, so violations of {\itshape size} should be exceptions.

Whether this constraint applies to the inner or the outer rect can be specified with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f}{set\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect} (see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}). Here is the call graph for this function\+:\nopagebreak

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f_a38975ea13e36de8e53391ce41d94bc0f} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Outer\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QRect \&}]{rect}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets the outer rect of this layout element. If the layout element is inside a layout, the layout sets the position and size of this layout element using this function.

Calling this function externally has no effect, since the layout will overwrite any changes to the outer rect upon the next replot.

The layout element will adapt its inner \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} by applying the margins inward to the outer rect.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_ae6aef2f7211ba6097c925dcd26008418_ae6aef2f7211ba6097c925dcd26008418}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!setRangeDrag@{setRangeDrag}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRangeDrag()}{setRangeDrag()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_ae6aef2f7211ba6097c925dcd26008418_ae6aef2f7211ba6097c925dcd26008418} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::set\+Range\+Drag (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Qt\+::\+Orientations}]{orientations}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets which axis orientation may be range dragged by the user with mouse interaction. What orientation corresponds to which specific axis can be set with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a648cce336bd99daac4a5ca3e5743775d_a648cce336bd99daac4a5ca3e5743775d}{set\+Range\+Drag\+Axes(\+QCPAxis \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}horizontal, QCPAxis \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}vertical)}. By default, the horizontal axis is the bottom axis (x\+Axis) and the vertical axis is the left axis (y\+Axis).

To disable range dragging entirely, pass {\ttfamily nullptr} as {\itshape orientations} or remove \doxylink{namespace_q_c_p_a2ad6bb6281c7c2d593d4277b44c2b037_a2ad6bb6281c7c2d593d4277b44c2b037a2c4432b9aceafb94000be8d1b589ef18}{QCP\+::i\+Range\+Drag} from \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5}{QCustom\+Plot\+::set\+Interactions}. To enable range dragging for both directions, pass {\ttfamily Qt\+::\+Horizontal \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} Qt\+::\+Vertical} as {\itshape orientations}.

In addition to setting {\itshape orientations} to a non-\/zero value, make sure \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5}{QCustom\+Plot\+::set\+Interactions} contains \doxylink{namespace_q_c_p_a2ad6bb6281c7c2d593d4277b44c2b037_a2ad6bb6281c7c2d593d4277b44c2b037a2c4432b9aceafb94000be8d1b589ef18}{QCP\+::i\+Range\+Drag} to enable the range dragging interaction.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a7960a9d222f1c31d558b064b60f86a31_a7960a9d222f1c31d558b064b60f86a31}{set\+Range\+Zoom}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a648cce336bd99daac4a5ca3e5743775d_a648cce336bd99daac4a5ca3e5743775d}{set\+Range\+Drag\+Axes}, \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_a775bdcb6329d44701aeaa6135b0e5265_a775bdcb6329d44701aeaa6135b0e5265}{QCustom\+Plot\+::set\+No\+Antialiasing\+On\+Drag} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a7960a9d222f1c31d558b064b60f86a31_a7960a9d222f1c31d558b064b60f86a31} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::set\+Range\+Zoom (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Qt\+::\+Orientations}]{orientations}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets which axis orientation may be zoomed by the user with the mouse wheel. What orientation corresponds to which specific axis can be set with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a9442cca2aa358405f39a64d51eca13d2_a9442cca2aa358405f39a64d51eca13d2}{set\+Range\+Zoom\+Axes(\+QCPAxis \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}horizontal, \+QCPAxis \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}vertical)}. By default, the horizontal axis is the bottom axis (x\+Axis) and the vertical axis is the left axis (y\+Axis).

To disable range zooming entirely, pass {\ttfamily nullptr} as {\itshape orientations} or remove \doxylink{namespace_q_c_p_a2ad6bb6281c7c2d593d4277b44c2b037_a2ad6bb6281c7c2d593d4277b44c2b037abee1e94353525a636aeaf0ba32b72e14}{QCP\+::i\+Range\+Zoom} from \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5}{QCustom\+Plot\+::set\+Interactions}. To enable range zooming for both directions, pass {\ttfamily Qt\+::\+Horizontal \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} Qt\+::\+Vertical} as {\itshape orientations}.

In addition to setting {\itshape orientations} to a non-\/zero value, make sure \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5_a5ee1e2f6ae27419deca53e75907c27e5}{QCustom\+Plot\+::set\+Interactions} contains \doxylink{namespace_q_c_p_a2ad6bb6281c7c2d593d4277b44c2b037_a2ad6bb6281c7c2d593d4277b44c2b037abee1e94353525a636aeaf0ba32b72e14}{QCP\+::i\+Range\+Zoom} to enable the range zooming interaction.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_ae29d6e9e54ebd981769c986e498ae118_ae29d6e9e54ebd981769c986e498ae118} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::set\+Range\+Zoom\+Axes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QList$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_axis}{QCPAxis}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} $>$}]{horizontal}{, }\item[{QList$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_axis}{QCPAxis}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} $>$}]{vertical}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

This method allows to set multiple axes up to react to horizontal and vertical zooming, and define specifically which axis reacts to which zoom orientation (irrespective of the axis orientation). \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_ae83d187b03fc6fa4f00765ad50cd3fc3_ae83d187b03fc6fa4f00765ad50cd3fc3}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!setRangeZoomFactor@{setRangeZoomFactor}}
\index{setRangeZoomFactor@{setRangeZoomFactor}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRangeZoomFactor()}{setRangeZoomFactor()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_ae83d187b03fc6fa4f00765ad50cd3fc3_ae83d187b03fc6fa4f00765ad50cd3fc3} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::set\+Range\+Zoom\+Factor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{factor}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

This is an overloaded member function, provided for convenience. It differs from the above function only in what argument(s) it accepts.

Sets both the horizontal and vertical zoom {\itshape factor}. \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a895d7ac745ea614e04056244b3c138ac_a895d7ac745ea614e04056244b3c138ac}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!setRangeZoomFactor@{setRangeZoomFactor}}
\index{setRangeZoomFactor@{setRangeZoomFactor}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setRangeZoomFactor()}{setRangeZoomFactor()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a895d7ac745ea614e04056244b3c138ac_a895d7ac745ea614e04056244b3c138ac} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::set\+Range\+Zoom\+Factor (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{horizontal\+Factor}{, }\item[{double}]{vertical\+Factor}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets how strong one rotation step of the mouse wheel zooms, when range zoom was activated with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a7960a9d222f1c31d558b064b60f86a31_a7960a9d222f1c31d558b064b60f86a31}{set\+Range\+Zoom}. The two parameters {\itshape horizontal\+Factor} and {\itshape vertical\+Factor} provide a way to let the horizontal axis zoom at different rates than the vertical axis. Which axis is horizontal and which is vertical, can be set with \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a9442cca2aa358405f39a64d51eca13d2_a9442cca2aa358405f39a64d51eca13d2}{set\+Range\+Zoom\+Axes}.

When the zoom factor is greater than one, scrolling the mouse wheel backwards (towards the user) will zoom in (make the currently visible range smaller). For zoom factors smaller than one, the same scrolling direction will zoom out. \Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!setSizeConstraintRect@{setSizeConstraintRect}}
\index{setSizeConstraintRect@{setSizeConstraintRect}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setSizeConstraintRect()}{setSizeConstraintRect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f_a361666cdcc6fbfd37344cc44be746b0f} 
void QCPLayout\+Element\+::set\+Size\+Constraint\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a_a0afb3e5773529e4bd20e448f81be4d2a}{Size\+Constraint\+Rect}}}]{constraint\+Rect}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Sets to which rect of a layout element the size constraints apply. Size constraints can be set via \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b_a5dd29a3c8bc88440c97c06b67be7886b}{set\+Minimum\+Size} and \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95_a74eb5280a737ab44833d506db65efd95}{set\+Maximum\+Size}.

The outer rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c_a2a32a12a6161c9dffbadeb9cc585510c}{outer\+Rect}) includes the margins (e.\+g. in the case of a \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect}{QCPAxis\+Rect} the axis labels), whereas the inner rect (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect}) does not.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::setup\+Full\+Axes\+Box (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{connect\+Ranges}{ = {\ttfamily false}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Convenience function to create an axis on each side that doesn\textquotesingle{}t have any axes yet and set their visibility to true. Further, the top/right axes are assigned the following properties of the bottom/left axes\+:

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item range (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_aebdfea5d44c3a0ad2b4700cd4d25b641_aebdfea5d44c3a0ad2b4700cd4d25b641}{QCPAxis\+::set\+Range}) \item range reversed (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_a2172fdb196b1a0dc3f40992fcad8e9e1_a2172fdb196b1a0dc3f40992fcad8e9e1}{QCPAxis\+::set\+Range\+Reversed}) \item scale type (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_adef29cae617af4f519f6c40d1a866ca6_adef29cae617af4f519f6c40d1a866ca6}{QCPAxis\+::set\+Scale\+Type}) \item tick visibility (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_ac891409315bc379e3b1abdb162c1a011_ac891409315bc379e3b1abdb162c1a011}{QCPAxis\+::set\+Ticks}) \item number format (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_ae585a54dc2aac662e90a2ca82f002590_ae585a54dc2aac662e90a2ca82f002590}{QCPAxis\+::set\+Number\+Format}) \item number precision (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_a21dc8023ad7500382ad9574b48137e63_a21dc8023ad7500382ad9574b48137e63}{QCPAxis\+::set\+Number\+Precision}) \item tick count of ticker (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_ticker_a47752abba8293e6dc18491501ae34008_a47752abba8293e6dc18491501ae34008}{QCPAxis\+Ticker\+::set\+Tick\+Count}) \item tick origin of ticker (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_ticker_ab509c7e500293bf66a8409f0d7c23943_ab509c7e500293bf66a8409f0d7c23943}{QCPAxis\+Ticker\+::set\+Tick\+Origin})\end{DoxyItemize}
Tick label visibility (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_a04ba16e1f6f78d70f938519576ed32c8_a04ba16e1f6f78d70f938519576ed32c8}{QCPAxis\+::set\+Tick\+Labels}) of the right and top axes are set to false.

If {\itshape connect\+Ranges} is true, the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_a0894084e4c16a1736534c4095746f910_a0894084e4c16a1736534c4095746f910}{range\+Changed} signals of the bottom and left axes are connected to the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_aebdfea5d44c3a0ad2b4700cd4d25b641_aebdfea5d44c3a0ad2b4700cd4d25b641}{QCPAxis\+::set\+Range} slots of the top and right axes. {\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_add049d464b9ef2ccdc638adc4ccb4aca_add049d464b9ef2ccdc638adc4ccb4aca} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d_a0d83360e05735735aaf6d7983c56374d}{Update\+Phase}}}]{phase}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

This method is called automatically upon replot and doesn\textquotesingle{}t need to be called by users of \doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect}{QCPAxis\+Rect}.

Calls the base class implementation to update the margins (see \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a929c2ec62e0e0e1d8418eaa802e2af9b_a929c2ec62e0e0e1d8418eaa802e2af9b}{QCPLayout\+Element\+::update}), and finally passes the \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4_a208effccfe2cca4a0eaf9393e60f2dd4}{rect} to the inset layout (\doxylink{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a949f803466619924c7018df4b511ae10_a949f803466619924c7018df4b511ae10}{inset\+Layout}) and calls its QCPInset\+Layout\+::update function.

\Hypertarget{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a93eeaa0c127d6d6fe8171b2455080262_a93eeaa0c127d6d6fe8171b2455080262}\index{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}!wheelEvent@{wheelEvent}}
\index{wheelEvent@{wheelEvent}!QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate@{QCPColorScaleAxisRectPrivate}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{wheelEvent()}{wheelEvent()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a93eeaa0c127d6d6fe8171b2455080262_a93eeaa0c127d6d6fe8171b2455080262} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::wheel\+Event (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{QWheel\+Event \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{event}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}, {\ttfamily [virtual]}}

This event gets called when the user turns the mouse scroll wheel while the cursor is over the layerable. Whether a cursor is over the layerable is decided by a preceding call to \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layout_element_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c_a62d60f1b0ee9bb23e38811d71586d79c}{select\+Test}.

The current pixel position of the cursor on the \doxylink{class_q_custom_plot}{QCustom\+Plot} widget is accessible via {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pos()}.

The {\ttfamily event-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}angle\+Delta()} indicates how far the mouse wheel was turned, which is usually +/-\/ 120 for single rotation steps. However, if the mouse wheel is turned rapidly, multiple steps may accumulate to one event, making the delta larger. On the other hand, if the wheel has very smooth steps or none at all, the delta may be smaller.

The default implementation does nothing.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde_aa9a7c807eaa4666870ac94aa6abc4dde}{mouse\+Press\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb_a9cd27ad8c5cfb49aefd9dbb30def4beb}{mouse\+Move\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_color_scale_axis_rect_private_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4_a6c89b988d3a0b93c0878f0ebdb5037f4}{mouse\+Release\+Event}, \doxylink{class_q_c_p_layerable_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81_a4171e2e823aca242dd0279f00ed2de81}{mouse\+Double\+Click\+Event} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_q_c_p_axis_rect_a5fc8460564e81dcc2a9343dc8bc1fe67_a5fc8460564e81dcc2a9343dc8bc1fe67} 
void QCPAxis\+Rect\+::zoom (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const QRectF \&}]{pixel\+Rect}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inherited]}}

Zooms in (or out) to the passed rectangular region {\itshape pixel\+Rect}, given in pixel coordinates.

All axes of this axis rect will have their range zoomed accordingly. If you only wish to zoom specific axes, use the overloaded version of this method.
